msg:Unforgettable Stay at Sofitel Hongqiao - Exceptional Hospitality by Christina
My family and I had the pleasure of staying at the Sofitel Hongqiao during our recent trip, and I must say, our experience was nothing short of outstanding. From the moment we arrived, we were greeted warmly and felt right at home. However, what truly made our stay memorable was the exceptional service provided by Christina at Front Desk.
Traveling with two young children can be a handful, but Christina went above and beyond to ensure our needs were met and our stay was comfortable. She was attentive and accommodating, offering helpful suggestions for family-friendly activities in the area and making sure our room was well-equipped for our little ones. Her genuine care and attention to detail made us feel like VIP guests throughout our entire visit.
The hotel itself was immaculate, with beautiful, modern d√©cor and top-notch amenities. Our room was spacious and spotlessly clean, providing a relaxing haven for our family after a long day of exploring. The on-site restaurant offered a delightful array of international cuisine, with options to satisfy even the pickiest of eaters (which was a relief for any parent!).
I wholeheartedly recommend the Sofitel Hongqiao to anyone seeking a luxurious and family-friendly stay in the area. The hotel's commitment to outstanding service, combined with Christina's exceptional hospitality, truly sets it apart as a premier destination for travelers. I look forward to our next visit and the opportunity to experience the unparalleled warmth and professionalism that this hotel offers.

Sofitel is now an environmentally friendly hotel and does not provide toothbrushes, toothpaste and combs. If you need it, you can directly ask the lobby for it. The overall service of the hotel is very good. I am impressed by the floor room cleaning staff on February 8, the female manager of the buffet breakfast restaurant on February 9, the boy who made egg rolls, the female chef of Ming Noodles, and the check-out. I chose a pot of Darjeeling black tea, my wife chose a pot of strawberry tea, the tea is fragrant, the pastries are delicious, the environment is elegant, the service is very good, and the waiters are very warm and friendly.

However, Sofitel's breakfast is also good. Basically every Sofitel has freshly squeezed watermelon juice and meringue rolls, and Xinhualian Sofitel is no exception. It meets my evaluation criteria for a five-star hotel buffet breakfast. Freshly squeezed The Sydney juice is also very rich, as well as the freshly made pancake fruit, the spicy meat and spicy sauce noodles and the small wontons in the Ming stall are all good. It's that Sofitel's breakfast has no French desserts except for some basic baguettes. Sofitel Hongqiao Xinhualian is both a business hotel and a resort hotel. Due to the epidemic and the off-season after the Spring Festival, the occupancy rate of the entire hotel is not very high, and there are not many people who use the buffet breakfast in the hotel. My wife was not feeling well, so I didn't eat breakfast. I told the restaurant, and the female manager of the restaurant readily agreed to let me choose and put it in the basin, and they packed it for me. I had a good breakfast, took two boxes of various breakfast foods and added a cup of American coffee before leaving. The restaurant is very reasonable and must be praised.
